<p><span style="font-size:12pt"><span style="font-family:Calibri,sans-serif"><strong><u>How to purchase Jazz Load form Jazz Cash account:</u></strong></span></span></p>

<p><span style="font-size:12pt"><span style="font-family:Calibri,sans-serif">*149#<span style="font-family:Wingdings">&agrave;</span>Please select Jazz Load units<span style="font-family:Wingdings">&agrave;</span>Enter Jazz cash MPIN<span style="font-family:Wingdings">&agrave;</span>confirmation SMS</span></span></p>

<ul>
	<li><span style="font-size:12pt"><span style="font-family:Calibri,sans-serif">Franchisee will dial *149# USSD String</span></span></li>
	<li><span style="font-size:12pt"><span style="font-family:Calibri,sans-serif">Franchisee will be asked to select Jazz Load units from the listed options or Franchisee can enter Jazz Load units of their choice, unit details are mentioned below in table</span></span></li>
	<li><span style="font-size:12pt"><span style="font-family:Calibri,sans-serif">Franchisee will need to enter the Jazz Cash MPIN</span></span></li>
	<li><span style="font-size:12pt"><span style="font-family:Calibri,sans-serif">Franchisee will receive confirmation SMS from 8558 of Jazz Cash deduction</span></span></li>
	<li><span style="font-size:12pt"><span style="font-family:Calibri,sans-serif">Franchisee will receive confirmation SMS from JAZZ for transferring of Jazz Load Balance</span></span></li>
</ul>

Complaint Description: <p><span style="font-size:14px">Incase if a customer visited retailer for CYN number activation and number is not activated and deduction has been made from EVC account of retailer and customer wants his money back (Reversal from customer to Retailer EVC)</span></p>

<p><span style="font-size:14px">Below is the handling of such cases&nbsp;</span></p>

<p><strong><span style="font-size:14px">System Based Auto Reversal:</span></strong></p>

<p><span style="font-size:14px">When retailer amount is deducted against <strong>CYN, Change of Sim,&nbsp;New SIM Sale, Data SIM Sale</strong> etc this amount will be automatically&nbsp;reversed back in 20 minutes Maximum as any of below cases or scenrios appears:</span></p>

<ul>
	<li><span style="font-size:14px">CYN (with Bundle or without bundle) /New Activation(with Bundle or without bundle) not process due to Tech reason or thumb not verified and amount deducts from EVC.</span></li>
	<li><span style="font-size:14px">Data SIM/MBB package plan, COS etc. Not process due to tech reason or thumb not verified and amount deducts from EVC</span></li>
</ul>

<p><span style="font-size:14px">In case retailer charged amount from customer andcustomer reverted back with the complaint that number is not yet activated in such scenerio customer need to check retailers respective franchise and visit there.&nbsp;</span></p>

ðŸ“‹ ENTRY: Retailers Balance Confiscation (More than 90 days)-EVC
------------------------------------------------------------
Main Header: RTG
Network Provider: Jazz
Complaint Description: <p>To <strong>Eliminate Inactive EVC Retailers</strong> in order to bring efficiency and improve customer experience, From today onwards all those retailers who did not use thier retailer EVC&nbsp;(load sim) from more than 90 days their balance will be confiscated (deleted) from EVC platform&nbsp;and SIMS will be blocked&nbsp;</p>

<p>&nbsp;</p>

<p><strong>Inactive Retailer Definition:</strong></p>

<p>An inactive retailer includes a retailer who has stopped purchasing load from Jazz and/or offering/re-selling Jazz load to customers or not performed any load related successful transaction activity (i.e., from Retailer to customer) within three (03) months period.</p>

<p>&nbsp;</p>

<p><strong>Inactive Retailers EVC Account Deletion</strong></p>

<p>Following steps will be taken against Inactive EVC Retailers:</p>

<ul style="list-style-type:disc">
	<li>The EVC Retailers will be guided/advised frequently to improve sale of load/top up to valued customers to improve customer experience else the contract will be terminated and EVC SIM will be blocked.</li>
</ul>

<ul style="list-style-type:disc">
	<li>Upon recommendation of Channel Planning team&nbsp;in the light of identification exercise, a notice will be sent to the Inactive EVC Retailers intimating that his contract will stand terminated <strong>after 48 hours</strong>.</li>
</ul>

<ul style="list-style-type:disc">
	<li>The said Notice may be sent to the Inactive EVC Retailer via SMS on his EVC SIM or MSISDN registered with Jazz.</li>
</ul>

<ul style="list-style-type:disc">
	<li>After lapse of 48 hours, if the EVC Retailer does do any load related activity, the EVC SIM of these inactive retailers will be blocked.</li>
</ul>

<p><strong>Handling of Blocked EVC Retailers:</strong></p>

<ul style="list-style-type:disc">
	<li>In case the blocked EVC Retailer again approaches Jazz/Franchisee, and request for activation of EVC SIM by assuring that he will improve his performance. Upon satisfaction of Franchisee, the EVC SIM can be activated by doing the following:</li>
</ul>

<p>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; (i) Fresh EVC Retailer Agreement will be signed with the Franchisee</p>

<p>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; (ii). Biometric verification through NADRA</p>

<p>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; (iii) Submission of other documents/assurances including copy of CNIC, etc.</p>

<p>&nbsp;</p>

<ul style="list-style-type:disc">
	<li>If the ECV Retailer fails to approach Jazz or Franchisee for reactivation of EVC SIM as per aforesaid criteria, within the period of 90 days from the date of blocking of EVC SIM, Jazz shall delete the account of the said Inactive EVC Retailer and may at its sole discretion, re-issue that EVC SIM to any other retailer.</li>
</ul>

<p>&nbsp;</p>

<p><strong>Balance Offloading Process</strong></p>

<ul>
	<li><strong>&nbsp;</strong>The outstanding dues will be adjusted from Inactive EVC Retailers&rsquo; account balance, and the remining amount will be offloaded and will be parked separately by the Finance team in a head.</li>
</ul>

<ul style="list-style-type:disc">
	<li>A detailed record of the offloaded balance will be maintained, including the EVC Retailers&rsquo; information, balance amount, and the date of offloading.</li>
</ul>

<ul style="list-style-type:disc">
	<li>Treatment of this offloaded amount will be devised as per best industry practice and reviewed from time to time to improve the same.</li>
</ul>

<ul style="list-style-type:disc">
	<li>The claims from ex-EVC Retailers will be entertained within a period of maximum three years from the date of offloading.</li>
</ul>

<ul style="list-style-type:disc">
	<li>This activity will be repeated every six months.</li>
</ul>

<p>&middot;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp; JazzCash Paypak debit card is auto enabled for all online/E-commerce payments within Pakistan (domestic platforms).</p>

<p>&middot;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp; We will reset CPS password of Franchise number if any Franchisee request for his CPS account password reset</p>

<p>&middot;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp; Franchise have an access of CPS portal</p>

<p>&middot;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp; We will reset CPS password for Franchise Calling CLI only after required verification through &ldquo;Reset Password&rdquo; option</p>

<p>&middot;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp; A password is a string of characters used to verify the identity of a user during the authentication process</p>

<p>&middot;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp; A password, sometimes called a passcode, is secret data, typically a string of characters, usually used to confirm a user&#39;s identity</p>

<p>&middot;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp; A good password is Include a mix of symbols, number and both upper- and lower-case letters</p>

<p>&middot;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp; Notification is sent from 8558</p>

<p>&middot;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp; In case Franchisee ask that I can select last pin when I receive temporary pin, in such cases we need to guide franchise that you need to have a new pin for your CPS you cannot use old pin</p>

ðŸ“‹ ENTRY: JazzCash â€“ Retailer â€“ NextGen Account Registration â€“ SOP
------------------------------------------------------------
Main Header: RTG
Network Provider: Jazz
Complaint Description: <p>&middot;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp; This SOP document will cover scenarios related with NextGen Account Registration</p>

<p>&middot;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp; New Business Opportunity for Retailers</p>

<p>&middot;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp; Pakistan&rsquo;s first ever &amp; only Digital Wallet for teenagers</p>

<p>&middot;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp; Retailer can Registered the NextGen Account through BVS Device</p>

<p>&middot;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp; All you need to do now, is have your guardian download the JazzCash Mobile app or is to visit your nearest JazzCash Retailer with your guardian &amp; you can have your very own Account Opened in under 5 minutes of time.</p>

<p>&middot;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp; Details to Register a Minor account, Guardian&rsquo;s CNIC &amp; JazzCash Account Number, Minor&rsquo;s CNIC/B-Form number &amp; date of issuance.</p>

<p>&middot;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp; JazzCash NextGen account gives you complete freedom to deposit, withdraw cash, make online payments, make QR payments or send money to friends</p>

<p>&middot;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp; One Guardian can get two minor accounts registered</p>

<p>&middot;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp; For Minors, only 1 account can be opened on 1 MSISDN. A Guardian can have 2 minor accounts registered in his name along with 1 standard JazzCash Account for himself</p>

<p>&middot;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp; When minor turns 18Minor gets SMS every week that his account will be blocked. To convert to adult, minor will visit any JazzCash retailer for biometric verification along with own CNIC details</p>

<p>&middot;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp; NextGen account Transaction limits are same as L1 account.</p>

<p>&middot;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp; Once the NextGen account is created, Customer will have to dial *786# from his/her registered number to create MPIN</p>

<p>&middot;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp; Process to migrate a Minor account to an adult (standard JazzCash), Minor may visit any JazzCash retailer &amp; provide their CNIC, Mobile number &amp; biometric verification to have their account migrated. The guardian does not have to accompany the minor.</p>

<p>&middot;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp; Retailer can transfer customer&#39;s Minor account from one number to another number</p>

<p>&middot;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp; Retailer gets Rs 80 commission for registering Minor account</p>

ðŸ“‹ ENTRY: JazzCash â€“ Retailer â€“ Tax Certificate - SOP 
------------------------------------------------------------
Main Header: RTG
Network Provider: Jazz
Complaint Description: <p>&middot;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp; In case retailer calls on 1344 and request for Tax Certificate</p>

<p>&middot;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp; we need to guide the retailer on call that Tax Certificate will be shared with regional teams of JazzCash, and it will be provided by Regional POC</p>

<p>&middot;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp; Retailer needs to request his JazzCash POC to get the tax Certificate</p>

<p>&middot;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp; Retailer Tax Certificate request will not be entertained at 1344</p>

<p>&middot;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp; A national retail sales tax is a consumption tax collected as a flat-rate tax on all sales from businesses to households.</p>

<p>&middot;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp; Tax certificate an official document which shows that the tax owed on an income, profit, property sale, etc. has been paid: This document confirms that the company holds a Tax Certificate</p>

<p>&middot;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp; The Federal Government of Pakistan (the Pakistani Government) has increased the general Sales Tax rate to 18% effective 14 February 2023.</p>

<p>&middot;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp; Tax Certificate for Retailer Receive in Email Address.</p>

<p>&middot;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp; If Retailer wants Tax Certificate in Hard Copy Franchise also gives a Tax certificate in Hard Copy</p>

<p>&middot;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp; Take your CNIC with you when visiting the retailer franchise</p>

ðŸ“‹ ENTRY: JazzCash â€“ Retailer â€“ Transaction Status â€“ SOP 
------------------------------------------------------------
Main Header: RTG
Network Provider: Jazz
Complaint Description: <p>&middot;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp; This process will cover call handling scenarios where Retailer is inquiring status of transaction.</p>

<p>&middot;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp; This process provides general guidelines to handle transaction Status related calls.</p>

<p>&middot;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp; This document has two sections that covers the call handling SOPs for respective transaction type as shown in below table.</p>

<table border="1" cellpadding="0" cellspacing="0">
	<tbody>
		<tr>
			<td style="vertical-align:top">
			<p><strong>Section</strong></p>
			</td>
			<td style="vertical-align:top">
			<p><strong>Transaction type</strong></p>
			</td>
			<td style="vertical-align:top">
			<p><strong>Description</strong></p>
			</td>
			<td style="vertical-align:top">
			<p><strong>Product &amp; Services</strong></p>
			</td>
		</tr>
		<tr>
			<td style="vertical-align:top">
			<p>Section 1</p>
			</td>
			<td style="vertical-align:top">
			<p>Outgoing Transactions</p>
			</td>
			<td style="vertical-align:top">
			<p>This section will cover processes to check status of all outgoing transactions for following products &amp; services.</p>
			</td>
			<td style="vertical-align:top">
			<p>Money Transfer (Cash-In, IBFT, CNIC, JazzCash to JazzLoad), UBP, Government Payments, MTAG, Loan Payments, Fee Payments, voucher/challan payments</p>
			</td>
		</tr>
		<tr>
			<td style="vertical-align:top">
			<p>Section 2</p>
			</td>
			<td style="vertical-align:top">
			<p>Incoming Transactions</p>
			</td>
			<td style="vertical-align:top">
			<p>This section will cover processes to check status of all incoming transactions of following products &amp; services.</p>
			</td>
			<td style="vertical-align:top">
			<p>Money Transfer (Cash Out, CNIC Receiving, Business Deposit) and Bank Cash In</p>
			</td>
		</tr>
	</tbody>
</table>

<p>&nbsp;</p>

<p>&middot;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp; Transaction status is a value mentioned in CPS which shows the state of a transaction.</p>

<p>&middot;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp; Agent can view status of a transaction using below navigation.</p>

<p>CPS &gt;&gt; transaction Tab &gt;&gt; Search by receipt No. &gt;&gt; Enter transaction ID &gt;&gt; Check transaction Status</p>

<p>&middot;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp; Agent can also check status of a transaction from Retailers transaction history via below navigation.</p>

<p>CPS &gt;&gt; Search MSISDN &gt;&gt; Click Review Transaction &gt;&gt; Enter Search Criteria &gt;&gt; Click Search &gt;&gt; Identify transaction from list &gt;&gt; Check Transaction Status</p>

<p>&middot;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp; Each transaction status value has specific meaning which helps agent to identify the outcome of transaction.</p>

<p>&middot;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp; Please refer to table 1.0 below for possible transaction statuses and their description.</p>

<table border="1" cellpadding="0" cellspacing="0" style="width:630px">
	<tbody>
		<tr>
			<td style="vertical-align:top">
			<p><strong>Transaction Status value</strong></p>
			</td>
			<td style="vertical-align:top">
			<p><strong>Description</strong></p>
			</td>
		</tr>
		<tr>
			<td style="vertical-align:top">
			<p>Complete</p>
			</td>
			<td style="vertical-align:top">
			<p>Transaction is successfully completed.</p>
			</td>
		</tr>
		<tr>
			<td style="vertical-align:top">
			<p>Expired</p>
			</td>
			<td style="vertical-align:top">
			<p>Transaction was not complete in specific time and gets expired. Balance will be returned to the Retailer account.</p>
			</td>
		</tr>
		<tr>
			<td style="vertical-align:top">
			<p>Cancelled</p>
			</td>
			<td style="vertical-align:top">
			<p>Transaction is not completed by Retailer.</p>
			</td>
		</tr>
		<tr>
			<td style="vertical-align:top">
			<p>Declined</p>
			</td>
			<td style="vertical-align:top">
			<p>Transaction is not completed by CPS due to specific error/limitation.</p>
			</td>
		</tr>
		<tr>
			<td style="vertical-align:top">
			<p>Authorized</p>
			</td>
			<td style="vertical-align:top">
			<p>Transaction was not completed within specific time. Retailer balance is reserved. This is an exception and will be catered as per scenario.</p>
			</td>
		</tr>
	</tbody>
</table>

<p>&nbsp;</p>

<p>&middot;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp; For transactions, where status is either Pending Authorized or Authorized, initial wait time is shared with Retailers.</p>

<p>&middot;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp; If transaction is in Authorized state and Retailer called after initial wait time, complaint needs to be made to update transaction state.</p>

<p>&middot;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp; Please refer to table 2.0 for service details.</p>

<p>&nbsp;</p>

<p><strong>Table 2.0</strong></p>

<table border="1" cellpadding="0" cellspacing="0">
	<tbody>
		<tr>
			<td style="vertical-align:top">
			<p><a name="_Hlk136191481"><strong>Transaction Status &ndash; Information</strong></a></p>
			</td>
			<td style="vertical-align:top">
			<p><strong>Value</strong></p>
			</td>
		</tr>
		<tr>
			<td style="vertical-align:top">
			<p>Channel</p>
			</td>
			<td style="vertical-align:top">
			<p>USSD, App, BVS Device</p>
			</td>
		</tr>
		<tr>
			<td style="vertical-align:top">
			<p>Retailer Profile</p>
			</td>
			<td style="vertical-align:top">
			<p>Jazz</p>
			</td>
		</tr>
		<tr>
			<td style="vertical-align:top">
			<p>Account Status</p>
			</td>
			<td style="vertical-align:top">
			<p>Active</p>
			</td>

<h1>&nbsp;</h1>

<p><a name="_Hlk135925583"><strong>Info Scenario </strong></a></p>

<p>&nbsp;</p>

<table border="1" cellpadding="0" cellspacing="0" style="width:624px">
	<tbody>
		<tr>
			<td style="vertical-align:top">
			<p><a name="_Hlk135925592"><strong>Scenario 1. Transaction Status &ndash; Scenarios</strong></a></p>
			</td>
		</tr>
		<tr>

Complaint Description: <p>&middot;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp; This SOP document will cover scenarios related BVS Device</p>

<p>&middot;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp; For first time, device will update App versions. Device/App updates may take 5 to 10 minutes depending on the internet connection</p>

<p>&middot;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp; An updated will be rolled out in a couple of days in which retailer will have to accept &amp; sign e-agreement on their first login</p>

<p>&middot;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp; The available JazzCash products on the retailer BVS Device are as follows:</p>

<p>&middot;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp; &nbsp;<strong>Send Money to CNIC</strong> &ndash; Depositing cash in the customer&rsquo;s JazzCash account</p>

<p>&middot;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp; <strong>Send Money to Bank Account &ndash; </strong>Send money to a bank account</p>

<p>&middot;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp; <strong>Cash-In &ndash; </strong>Depositing cash in the customer&rsquo;s JazzCash account</p>

<p>&middot;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp; <strong>Cash-Out</strong> &ndash; Withdrawal of cash from the customer&rsquo;s JazzCash account</p>

<p>&middot;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp; <strong>Cash-Out from CNIC &ndash; </strong>Withdrawal of cash from the customer&rsquo;s CNIC</p>

<p>&middot;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp; <strong>Biometric Complaint Management &ndash; </strong>Edit the receiver CNIC number</p>

<p>&middot;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp; <strong>New Account Registration</strong> &ndash; Opening a Jazz Cash account at the request of the customer</p>

<p>&middot;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp; <strong>Account Limit Upgrade &ndash; </strong>Customer&#39;s /merchants JazzCash account limit will be changed from L0 to L1 for merchant M0, to M1</p>

<p>&middot;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp; <strong>Reset MPIN &ndash; </strong>To reset the customer&#39;s JazzCash account MPIN</p>

<p>&middot;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp; <strong>Dormancy Removal &ndash; </strong>Activating the customer&#39;s JazzCash Account from Dormant to Active</p>

<p>&middot;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp; <strong>Home Remittance account &ndash; </strong>Opening a Home Remittance account at the request of the customer</p>

<p>&middot;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp; <strong>Minor Account -</strong> Opening a Minor account at the request of the</p>

<p>&middot;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp; <strong>Change of MSISDN - </strong>Transferring a customer&#39;s JazzCash account from one number to another Number</p>

ðŸ“‹ ENTRY: JazzCash â€“ Retailer â€“ Cash In â€“ SOP
------------------------------------------------------------
Main Header: RTG
Network Provider: Jazz
Complaint Description: <p>&middot;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp; This SOP document will cover scenarios related Cash In/Cash deposit.</p>

<p>&middot;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp; Retailer can send amount to Customer JazzCash account upon customer request. Customer give physical cash to retailer and retailer transfer electronic funds to customer&rsquo;s account.</p>

<p>&middot;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp; Any person can send money to a Mobile Account from any JazzCash Agent across Pakistan</p>

<p>&middot;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp; To receive funds in JazzCash, customer provide mobile number and physical cash to retailer, retailer transfers respective amount in customer&rsquo;s JazzCash account. Customer receives a confirmation SMS on mobile number.</p>

<p><a name="_Hlk139326304">&middot;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp; Funds transfer via Cash-In transaction are posted in real time.</a></p>

<p>&middot;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp; Minimum Cash-In amount is 50 Rs.</p>

<p>&middot;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp; Maximum Cash-In amount is as per customer account limit.</p>

<p>&middot;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp; In case retailer calls and wanted to ask MSISDN of any transaction performed by him/her, agent will not share any MSISDN on call. However, in order to facilitate retailer, agent can ask the retailer to share the customer&rsquo;s MSISDN and reply in &quot;Yes&quot; or &quot;No&quot; whether the MSISDN shared by retailer is correct or incorrect.</p>

<p>&middot;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp; Cash-In cannot be performed by retailer in customer L0 account via USSD or retailer App.</p>

<p>&middot;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp; Retailer can perform Cash-In on L0 via BVS device where customer will get BVS verified during cash-in transaction. Customer&rsquo;s account will be upgraded to L1 and Cash-In transaction will be completed. Funds will be transferred to customer account in real time.</p>

<p>&middot;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp; Agent must confirm transaction date, time and amount if retailer wants to verify/confirm any transaction from helpline.</p>

<p>&middot;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp; Retailer cannot reverse a Cash In transaction.</p>

<p>&middot;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp; Cash-In transaction has service charges as per Cash-In amount. Please refer to below table for details.</p>

<p>&middot;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp; Cash-In fee is charged to customer and will not be deducted from retailer&rsquo;s account.&nbsp;</p>

	<li>Tax percentage is charged on the fee, not the Cash-In amount.</li>
	<li>The fee and tax will be deducted from the Cash-In amount, and the remaining balance will be deposited into the customer&#39;s account.</li>

	<li>Please guide agent to inform the customer that if they wish to have a specific amount deposited into their account, they can Cash-In an additional amount equal to the fee + tax (Total Deduction), as explained in the example above.</li>
	<li>The customer will receive an SMS showing the original/exact amount deposited by the retailer. However, the customer&#39;s account will be credited with the amount after deducting the fee + tax.</li>
	<li>Customer should pay only the original/exact amount showing in the SMS. For reference, see highlighted value in below SMS. &nbsp;</li>
	<li>Dear Customer, Rs. XXXXX.XX have been deposited in your JazzCash Account, Balance: Rs. XXXXX. XX. TID: xxxxxxxxxxxxx. Charges are applicable.</li>
</ul>

<p>&middot;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp; Retailer SMS:<strong> </strong>TID xxxxxxxxxxxx. Cash-In of Rs. xxxx.xxx in xxxxxxxxxx is successful. Commission xx.xx, Fee: Rs.xx.xx, Collect: Rs.xxxx.xxx, Available Balance: Rs. xxxx. xx.</p>

ðŸ“‹ ENTRY: JazzCash â€“ Retailer â€“ Business Deposit â€“ SOP
------------------------------------------------------------
Main Header: RTG
Network Provider: Jazz
Complaint Description: <p>&middot;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp; This SOP document will cover scenarios related Business Deposit</p>

<p>&middot;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp; The service is free of charge for retailers with transaction Limit 500,000 per transaction (1.5 Million per day)</p>

<p>&middot;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp; JazzCash retailers initiate Business Deposit request through JazzCash Retailer App &amp; USSD (*787)</p>

<p>&middot;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp; The &lsquo;Request ID&rsquo; generated is then used to deposit cash into their MWs through <strong>UBL/MCB/MMBL/Alfalah Bank &amp; HBL</strong>.</p>

<p>&middot;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp; When performing business deposit retailer need to fill deposit slip and submit in bank. This deposit slip is available in franchise and bank from which business deposit is performed</p>

<p>&middot;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp; In addition to this, HBL e-deposit integration now enables JazzCash retailers to deposit funds via HBL App directly into JazzCash Retailer MW, without visiting the bank</p>

<p>&middot;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp; Currently Retailer e-deposit (HBL) is only available through Retailer USSD</p>

<p>&middot;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp; Please note that this facility is only available on HBL App / Portal, Retailer cannot avail this facility form HBL Bank branches</p>

<p><a name="_Hlk139326304">&middot;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp; Retailer Business Deposit transaction can be identified in CPS by transaction type &ldquo;Business Cash In&rdquo; in transaction details</a></p>

------------------------------------------------------------
Main Header: RTG
Network Provider: Jazz
Complaint Description: <p>&middot;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp; This SOP document will cover scenarios related JazzCash Retailer App</p>

<p>&middot;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp; Old Jazz Cash Retailer App have stopped working effective 30thJune 2020.</p>

<p>&middot;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp; Jazz cash retailer application, agent guide that Retailer new application is an android based application for Jazz cash only and available on the Google Play store</p>

<p>&middot;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp; Users will move to Latest Jazz Cash Retailer App through forced update (currently 17.0).</p>

<p>&middot;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp; All new users will download the app through Google Play store</p>

<p>&middot;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp; Only one MSISDN/IMEI can register against Retailer App</p>

<p>&middot;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp; Sim Should be in sim Slot 1 and No other Jazz/JazzCash app has been registered in cell phone</p>

<p>&middot;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp; Transaction will not process via Retailer App for L0 accounts (Non-BVS)</p>

<p><a name="_Hlk139326304">&middot;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp; Transaction via JazzCash Retailer App</a></p>

<p>&sect;&nbsp; Cash-In</p>

<p>&sect;&nbsp; Cash-Out</p>

<p>&sect;&nbsp; Postpaid Bill Payments</p>

<p>&sect;&nbsp; Utility Bill Payments (UBP)</p>

<p>&sect;&nbsp; Send IBFT</p>

<p>&sect;&nbsp; Electricity</p>

<p>&sect;&nbsp; Gas</p>

<p>&sect;&nbsp; Internet Payments</p>

<p>&sect;&nbsp; Water</p>

<p>&sect;&nbsp; Transfer to Agent</p>

<p>&sect;&nbsp; Transfer to Franchise</p>

<p>&sect;&nbsp; Business Deposit</p>

<p>&sect;&nbsp; Business Deposit Status Report</p>

<p>&sect;&nbsp; Change MPIN</p>

<p>&middot;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp; Report could be generated for Current day/ Last 7 days / Last 30 days / Custom date selection</p>

<p>&middot;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp; Real Time commission &amp; Tax deducted visibility with the export option</p>

<p>&middot;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp; Retailer also provides a physical application &amp; scanned CNIC copy to have it uploaded on agent app portal which is done through field teams (RDO TSS etc.). ðŸ“‹ ENTRY: JazzCash â€“ Retailer â€“ Cash Out â€“ SOP
------------------------------------------------------------
Main Header: RTG
Network Provider: Jazz
Complaint Description: <p>&middot;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp; This SOP document will cover scenarios related Cash Out</p>

<p>&middot;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp; Retailer can Withdraw amount to Customer JazzCash account</p>

<p>&middot;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp; Customer can withdraw cash from his Mobile Account from any JazzCash Agent across Pakistan</p>

<p>&middot;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp; To withdraw cash, Customer provide his Mobile number to the Agent, confirm withdrawal with his MPIN and collect cash</p>

<p><a name="_Hlk139326304">&middot;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp; Retailer Withdraw amount to Retailer account are posted in real time.</a></p>

<p>&middot;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp; Retailer can performed Cash Out as per customer account limit</p>

<p>&middot;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp; Retailer can check last 5 transaction via USSD through</p>

<p>&middot;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp; Transactions history are updated real time.</p>

<p>&middot;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp; In case retailer calls and wanted to ask any MSISDN related information against his previous transactions, we will not confirm any MSISDN on call, in order to facilitate we only ask the retailer to confirm the MSISDN and will reply in &quot;Yes&quot; or &quot;No&quot; accordingly</p>

<p>&middot;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp; Cash Out cannot be performed by retailer in customer L0 account</p>

<p>&middot;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp; Retailer Check cash Out Transaction in CPS to Ask Retailer for transaction date, time and amount</p>

<p>&middot;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp; Customer Cannot Reversed Cash Out transaction</p>

<p>&middot;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp; Cash Out Charges, Charge to only Customer</p>

<p>&middot;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp; This Transaction in only for Franchise</p>

<p>&middot;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp; Franchise can now purchase Jazz Load from their excessive Jazz Cash account balance</p>

<p>&middot;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp; Jazz Load can be purchased 24/7 as there is no need to wait for banks to open and working days to come to get Jazz Load from (PMCL) Pakistan Mobile Communication Limited</p>

<p>&middot;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp; Retail channel complaints for having excessive Jazz cash balance can be resolved since DO can send Jazz Load to retailers against their excessive Jazz Cash and then buy Jazz Load (OTAR) from same Jazz Cash from PMCL</p>

<p>&middot;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp; Jazz Load will be available to franchises within no time since there is no approval mechanism</p>

<p>&middot;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp; Retailer JazzCash to JazzLoad transaction can be identified in CPS by transaction type &ldquo;Donations&rdquo; in transaction details</p>

<p>&middot;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp; Franchisee can enter Jazz Load units of their choice, unit details are mentioned below in table</p>

ðŸ“‹ ENTRY: JazzCash â€“ Retailer - MPIN - SOP 
------------------------------------------------------------
Main Header: RTG
Network Provider: Jazz
Complaint Description: <p>&middot;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp; Mobile Personal Identification Number (MPIN) is a 4-digit security code that is required to login to JazzCash account or to authorize any transactions.</p>

<p>&middot;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp; MPIN status has 4 values = Normal, Locked, Pending Active</p>

<table border="1" cellpadding="0" cellspacing="0">
	<tbody>
		<tr>
			<td style="vertical-align:top">
			<p>PIN Status Value</p>
			</td>
			<td style="vertical-align:top">
			<p>Description</p>
			</td>
			<td style="vertical-align:top">
			<p>Action Required</p>
			</td>
		</tr>
		<tr>
			<td style="vertical-align:top">
			<p>Normal</p>
			</td>
			<td style="vertical-align:top">
			<p>MPIN is set and in active state</p>
			</td>
			<td style="vertical-align:top">
			<p>&middot;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp; Guide Retailer to use current MPIN</p>

			<p>&middot;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp; In case Retailer does not remember MPIN, Reset MPIN (system navigation)</p>
			</td>
		</tr>
		<tr>
			<td style="vertical-align:top">
			<p>Locked</p>
			</td>
			<td style="vertical-align:top">
			<p>MPIN is locked due to 3 wrong entries</p>
			</td>
			<td style="vertical-align:top">
			<p>Reset MPIN (system navigation)</p>
			</td>
		</tr>
		<tr>
			<td style="vertical-align:top">
			<p>Pending Active</p>
			</td>
			<td style="vertical-align:top">
			<p>MPIN has been reset and temporary MPIN has been generated by system. MPIN setup is required by Retailer</p>
			</td>
			<td style="vertical-align:top">
			<p>Ask if Retailer has temporary MPIN.</p>

			<p>If yes, refer to 2.2</p>

			<p>If no, Reset MPIN (system navigation)</p>
			</td>
		</tr>
	</tbody>
</table>

<p>&nbsp;</p>

<p>&middot;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp; MPIN can be changed via USSD, App, however can only be reset via Helpline&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;</p>

<p>&middot;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp; Notification is sent from 8558.</p>

<p>&sect;&nbsp; 8558 SMS number should not be in screened numbers, blocked or black-list numbers.</p>

<p>&sect;&nbsp; Phone memory should not be full.</p>

<p>&middot;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp; Agent must not reset MPIN multiple times during same call.</p>

<p>&middot;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp; If Retailer calls for MPIN reset, if Retailer denies receiving MPIN on the same calls, ask Retailer to wait for 15 minutes.</p>

<p>&middot;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp; MPIN should be kept secret, and not to share with anyone.</p>

<p>&middot;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp; Agent must guide Retailer how-to processes of Setting up, changing, after MPIN is reset.</p>

<p>&middot;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp; If mother name is not available in CPS then agent will ask CNIC expiry and if CNIC expiry is not updated in system or Retailer is not having ID card then we need 1344 agent will check mother name from NADRA link</p>

ðŸ“‹ ENTRY: JazzCash â€“ Retailer â€“ Outgoing IBFT â€“ SOP
------------------------------------------------------------
Main Header: RTG
Network Provider: Jazz
Complaint Description: <p>&middot;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp; This SOP document will cover scenarios related Retailer Outgoing IBFT</p>

<p>&middot;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp; Retailer can send amount any bank account.</p>

<p>&middot;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp; To add other bank account for Outgoing IBFT, the Bank name should exist in JazzCash IBFT list.</p>

<p>&middot;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp; Retailer only performs Outgoing IBFT Transaction, Incoming IBFT transaction is not allow to Retailer</p>

<p>&middot;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp; IBFT is &#39;Inter Bank Fund Transfer&#39;, it means to transfer funds from your Retailer account to any other bank account of beneficiary.</p>

<p>&middot;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp; Through JazzCash Retailer Account, you can transfer money to any Bank Account smoothly</p>

<p>&middot;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp; Retailer Outgoing IBFT service is not free of cost, fund transfer charges are applicable as per sending amount</p>

<p><a name="_Hlk139326304">&middot;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp; Retailer Outgoing IBFT transaction can be identified in CPS by transaction type &ldquo;Outgoing IBFT&rdquo; in transaction details</a></p>

<p>&middot;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp; &nbsp;Retailer Cannot Reversed this transaction</p>

ðŸ“‹ ENTRY: JazzCash â€“ Retailer â€“ Pakistan Railway â€“ SOP
------------------------------------------------------------
Main Header: RTG
Network Provider: Jazz
Complaint Description: <p>&middot;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp; This SOP document will cover scenarios related Pakistan Railway</p>

<p>&middot;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp; Customer will visit Railways Application for booking of tickets</p>

<p>&middot;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp; And also, visit railways website https://www.pakrail.gov.pk/ for booking of tickets</p>

<p>&sect;&nbsp; Customer will click on &ldquo;go for E-ticket&rdquo;</p>

<p>&sect;&nbsp; Customer will select following data on the website</p>

<p>&sect;&nbsp; Departure Date</p>

<p>&sect;&nbsp; Train</p>

<p>&sect;&nbsp; From Station</p>

<p>&sect;&nbsp; To Station</p>

<p>&sect;&nbsp; Enter Captcha Code</p>

<p>&middot;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp; Customers cannot book train tickets prior to 12 hours before the departure time (Means, customer has to book tickets at least 13 hours or more before the departure time)</p>

<p><a name="_Hlk139326304">&middot;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp; Once customer is registered and seat is selected, if customer will select payment option as Jazz Cash payment process through voucher Payments then it will be paid through retailer</a></p>

<p>&middot;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp; Customer will enter his/her mobile account number to receive voucher code</p>

<p>&middot;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp; Customer will receive voucher code via SMS and will be displayed on the website also</p>

<p>&middot;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp; Ticket will be confirmed but if train departure time is within 12 hours then the voucher will be cancelled and customer will not be able to pay</p>

<p>&middot;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp; Customer will visit nearest Jazz Cash agent for Payment</p>

ðŸ“‹ ENTRY: JazzCash â€“ Retailer â€“ Postpaid Bill â€“ SOP
------------------------------------------------------------
Main Header: RTG
Network Provider: Jazz
Complaint Description: <p>&middot;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp; This SOP document will cover scenarios related Retailer Postpaid Bill</p>

<p>&middot;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp; POSTPAID is a billing model where you are charged for your service usage and subscriptions, the month after you have utilized the services.</p>

<p>&middot;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp; The postpaid connection is one in which you first avail the services and thereafter pay the price for it.</p>

<p>&middot;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp; There are no additional charges for postpaid bill payment through JazzCash retailer. Retailers if caught charging customers will be blacklisted.</p>

<p>&middot;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp; Postpaid billing is when you pay for your service after you use it.</p>

<p>&middot;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp; postpaid plans are paid at the end of the month.</p>

<p>&middot;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp; JazzCash services are available 24/7 so Retailer can pay customers bills at any time of the day or night</p>

<p>&middot;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp; The &ldquo;Mobile Postpaid&rdquo; service allows retailers to pay mobile postpaid bills on behalf of the customers.</p>

<p>&middot;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp; Prior to paying postpaid bills, the retailer must verify the number and amount with the customer to avoid an incorrect payment</p>

<p><a name="_Hlk139326304">&middot;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp; Retailer Postpaid Bill transaction can be identified in CPS by transaction type &ldquo;Indigo Bill Payment&rdquo; in transaction details</a></p>

ðŸ“‹ ENTRY: JazzCash â€“ Retailer â€“ USSD Menu *787# â€“ SOP
------------------------------------------------------------
Main Header: RTG
Network Provider: Jazz
Complaint Description: <p>&middot;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp; This SOP document will cover scenarios related USSD Menu *787#</p>

<p>&middot;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp; *787# menu is just for JazzCash Retailer users</p>

<p>&middot;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp; There are no additional charges of *787# menu</p>

<p>&middot;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp; The available JazzCash products on the retailer USSD menu * 787# are as follows:</p>

<p>&middot;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp; &nbsp;<strong>Cash-In</strong> &ndash; Depositing cash in the customer&rsquo;s JazzCash account</p>

<p>&middot;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp; &nbsp;<strong>Cash-Out</strong> &ndash; Withdrawal of cash from the customer&rsquo;s JazzCash account</p>

<p>&middot;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp; &nbsp;<strong>Send Money</strong> &ndash; Send money to a mobile or bank account</p>

<p>&middot;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp; &nbsp;<strong>Pay Bills</strong> &ndash; Pay utility bills, such as: IESCO, KESC, SNGPL and WASA</p>

<p>&middot;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp; <strong>&nbsp;Payments</strong> &ndash; Loan Payments, M-Tag Recharge, Donations etc.</p>

<p>&middot;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp; <strong>&nbsp;Mobile Post</strong>paid &ndash; Jazz customers&rsquo; postpaid bill payments</p>

<p>&middot;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp; <strong>&nbsp;Transfer Funds to Agent</strong> &ndash; Transfer funds to a retailer (franchise only)</p>

<p>&middot;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp; <strong>&nbsp;Manage Account</strong> &ndash; Manage MPIN, Check Balance, Mini statements etc.</p>

<p>&middot;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp; <strong>&nbsp;Register MA</strong> &ndash; Register the customer&rsquo;s level 0 account</p>

<p>&middot;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp; <strong>&nbsp;Retailer Deposit</strong> &ndash; Retailers self-deposit amount to JazzCash account via bank</p>

<p>&middot;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp; <strong>Debit Card Order </strong>&ndash; for order a debit card</p>

ðŸ“‹ ENTRY: JazzCash â€“ Retailer â€“ Utility Bill â€“ SOP
------------------------------------------------------------
Main Header: RTG
Network Provider: Jazz
Complaint Description: <p>&middot;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp; This SOP document will cover scenarios related Utility Bill</p>

<p>&middot;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp; Paying Bills through JazzCash Retailer Account is simple and easy! All you need to do is follow simple steps to pay Bills</p>

<p>&middot;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp; Retailer can pay all your Utility Bills such as Electricity, Gas, Telephone or Water bills through JazzCash Retailer Account, USSD or Bulk Bill Payment Portal</p>

<p>&middot;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp; Below are the UBP companies of which Retailer can pay bill</p>

<table border="1" cellpadding="0" cellspacing="0">
	<tbody>
		<tr>

			</td>

			</td>
			<td style="vertical-align:top">
			<p><strong>Telephone</strong></p>
			</td>
			<td style="vertical-align:top">
			<p><strong>Internet</strong></p>
			</td>
		</tr>
		<tr>
			<td style="vertical-align:top">
			<p>FESCO<br />
			GEPCO<br />
			HESCO<br />
			IESCO<br />
			K-ELECTRIC<br />
			LESCO<br />
			MEPCO<br />
			NIZAM ENERGY<br />

			QESCO<br />
			SEPCOS</p>
			</td>
			<td style="vertical-align:top">

			SSGC</p>

			<p>&nbsp;</p>
			</td>
			<td style="vertical-align:top">
			<p>BWASA<br />
			FWASA<br />
			GWASA<br />
			HYDERABAD WASA<br />
			KWSB<br />
			LWASA<br />
			MWASA<br />
			PHED HARIPUR<br />
			RWASA<br />
			WSSC SWAT<br />
			WSSP</p>
			</td>
			<td style="vertical-align:top">
			<p>NAYATEL<br />
			OPTIX<br />
			PTCL EVO POSTPAID<br />
			PTCL EVO PREPAID<br />
			TRANSWORLD<br />
			WATEEN<br />
			WORLDCALL</p>
			</td>
			<td style="vertical-align:top">
			<p>PTCL LANDLINE<br />
			PTCL VFONE PREPAID</p>

			<p>&nbsp;</p>
			</td>
		</tr>
	</tbody>
</table>

<p>&nbsp;</p>

<p>&middot;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp; Retailer will select desired UBP Company and enter consumer number/reference number and fetch bill amount will be auto fetched, after entering MPIN bill will be paid</p>

<p>&middot;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp; The scanner can be used through the JazzCash Retailer app where selecting the barcode icon can allow users to scan their relevant bill barcode and instantly fetch their bill details for payment</p>

<p>&middot;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp; The scanner can be used to scan a barcode through your phones camera</p>

<p>&middot;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp; A Retailer should not be able to pay more than Rs. 100,000 bill</p>

<p>&middot;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp; Retailer can receive 4.96 rupees commission per utility bill Transaction</p>

<p><a name="_Hlk139326304">&middot;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp; Retailer Utility Bill transaction can be identified in CPS by transaction type &ldquo;Utility Bill Payment&rdquo; in transaction details</a></p>

<p><a name="_Hlk145581832">&middot;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp; If Retailer call and complaint about bill paid within due date but amount deducted more than Bill amount, Helpline agent after consulting system need to guide Retailer to wait for next month bill as it will be adjusted in next month bill</a></p>

<p>&middot;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp; If Retailer pay bill and amount is deducted twice inform Retailer that extra amount will be reversed within 24 hours.</p>

<p><strong>Utility Bill Payment &ndash; Bill Paid against Wrong Reference Number:</strong></p>

<p>&middot;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp; Retailer pay against wrong reference number agent will inform Retailer that bill is paid and no reversal is possible and inform Retailer to coordinate with relevant billing company.</p>

<p><strong>Utility Bill Payment &ndash; Unable to Pay Bill:</strong></p>

<p>&middot;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp; If Retailer is paying bill but is unable to pay bill due to any valid error agent will ask Retailer whether bill is received in hard copy or not.</p>

<p>&middot;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp; If bill is not received in hard copy agent will inform Retailer to wait for the bill to be received in hard copy</p>

<p>&middot;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp; If bill is received in hard copy agent will simply forward complaint (Refer to JazzCash &ndash; Retailer &ndash; Utility Bill &ndash; Complaint Management)</p>

<p><strong>Utility Bill Payment &ndash; Bill Paid in Due Date:</strong></p>

<p>&middot;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp; If Retailer pay bill in due date and bill is received with arrears next month agent will forward complaint (Refer to JazzCash &ndash; Retailer &ndash; Utility Bill &ndash; Complaint)</p>

<p><strong>Utility Bill Payment &ndash; Amount Deducted Twice</strong></p>

<p>&middot;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp; If Retailer pay bill and amount is deducted twice inform Retailer that extra amount will be reversed within 24 hours.</p>

<p>&middot;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp; If amount is not reversed in 24 hours agent will forward complaint (Refer to JazzCash &ndash; Retailer &ndash; Utility Bill &ndash; Complaint).</p>

<p><strong>Utility Bill Payment &ndash; Amount Deducted More Than Bill Amount:</strong></p>

<p>&middot;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp; If Retailer pay bill and amount paid is greater than bill amount inform Retailer that amount will be adjusted in next bill if not adjusted than proceed with complaint registration (Refer to JazzCash &ndash; Retailer &ndash; Utility Bill &ndash; Complaint)</p>

<p><strong>Utility Bill Payment &ndash; Bill Paid After Due Date:</strong></p>

<p>&middot;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp; If Retailer pay bill late (after due date) and transaction is completed and Retailer is complaining that bill is not updated just inform Retailer to contact with relevant billing company.</p>

<p><strong>Utility Bill Payment &ndash; Bill Paid Wrong by System Issue:</strong></p>

<p><a name="_Hlk148540797">&middot;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp; If Retailer calls and say that he was paying current month bill but previous month bill got paid by system issue agent will inform Retailer that bill amount will be adjusted in next month bill</a>.</p>

<p>&middot;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp; If next month bill is received without adjustment agent will forward complaint registration (Refer to JazzCash &ndash; Retailer &ndash; Utility Bill &ndash; Complaint)</p>

<p><strong>Utility Bill Payment &ndash; Bill Paid Against Two Channel:</strong></p>

<p><a name="_Hlk148541633">&middot;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp; If Retailer pay bill from any other bank and same bill is paid again from JazzCash</a>, agent will just inform Retailer that the bill will be adjusted in next month bill</p>

<p>&middot;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp; &nbsp;If Retailer wants adjustment right now, then agent will inform Retailer to just contact relevant billing company.</p>

<p>&middot;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp; If next month bill is received without adjustment agent will forward complaint registration (Refer to JazzCash &ndash; Retailer &ndash; Utility Bill &ndash; Complaint)</p>

<p><strong>Proof of Utility Bill Payment:&nbsp; </strong></p>

<p>&middot;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp; Utility Bill was paid but the new bill showing arrears, and billing companies are asking for proof of utility bill payment via JazzCash.</p>

<p>&middot;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp; In case Retailer came with below complaint provide the below details (mentioned in table) to him/her on call in order to facilitate by checking CPS</p>

<p>&middot;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp; Agent need to request the Retailer to note down the details carefully and share that with UBP company</p>

<p>&sect;&nbsp; Receipt No.:</p>

<p>&sect;&nbsp; Status:</p>

<p>&sect;&nbsp; Date and time:</p>

<p>&sect;&nbsp; Initiator:</p>

<p>&sect;&nbsp; Credit Party (which is utility bill company):</p>

<p>&sect;&nbsp; Amount Due</p>

<p>&sect;&nbsp; Amount Paid</p>

<p>&sect;&nbsp; Bill reference number</p>

<p>Bulk Bill portal specifications:</p>

<p>&middot;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp; Upto 50 bills payment at a time through portal, rest of the bill payment mechanism is as per existing process except for bulk payments</p>

<p>&middot;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp; Max 100K ticket size per bill</p>

<p>&middot;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp; Cash In Cash Out as per existing process</p>

<p>&middot;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp; Bill payment details can be entered on the portal or can also be uploaded on the portal through the sample sheet provided</p>

<p>&middot;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp; Commissions remain the same</p>

<p>Issues</p>

<p>&middot;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp; Portal login issues &ndash; if portal is down there will be a message displayed on the website</p>

<p>&middot;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp; Incorrect user name password</p>

<p>&middot;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp; All portal related issues are to be raised with ITFS, password reset/ ID deletion requests are also to be fixed by ITFS</p>

ðŸ“‹ ENTRY: JazzCash Retailer â€“ Account Closure - SOP
------------------------------------------------------------
Main Header: RTG
Network Provider: Jazz
Complaint Description: <p>&middot;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp; JazzCash Retailer account is just like a Business account. Like any bank account, Retailer has a legal right to close JazzCash Retailer account.</p>

<p>&middot;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp; Retailer can request for JazzCash Retailer account closure by visiting Jazz Experience center, franchise.</p>

<p>&middot;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp; Agent must check account status (system navigation) before inform to Retailer account closure request.&nbsp;</p>

<p>&middot;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp; Account status must be in Active, Pending Active.</p>

<p>&middot;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp; For Suspended state due to CNIC expiry, guide to Retailer visit Franchise, Jazz Experience center and lodged Complaint for activation or Closure</p>

<p>&middot;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp; For Suspended state due to fraud, guide the Retailer to visit Franchise, or Jazz Experience Center for account closure or activation.</p>

<p>&middot;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp; For Frozen state, guide Retailer to visit Jazz Experience Center, franchise for account closure.</p>

<p>&middot;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp; Account closed if there is any balance available in account, but firstly guide to Retailer account balance send any Franchise account then Retailer has to close his Jazz Cash Retailer account</p>

<p>&middot;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp; The franchise or jazz experience center will Inform to the retailer, how many days will your JazzCash Retailer account close</p>

<p>&middot;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp; JazzCash Retailer account is not transferred to any other number</p>

<p>&middot;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp; If a retailer wants to create an account at another number, they must first close their account</p>

<p>&middot;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp; But if you want to create an account on another number and don&#39;t want to get your account close, then you can create another account on another CNIC number.</p>

<p>&middot;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp; Please refer to below table 1.0 for service details.</p>

ðŸ“‹ ENTRY: JazzCash Retailer â€“ Account Opening â€“ SOP
------------------------------------------------------------
Main Header: RTG
Network Provider: Jazz
Complaint Description: <p>&middot;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp; Retailer call on helpline and wanted to ask details about Account opening process agent to follow below statement:</p>

<p>&middot;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp; JazzCash Retailer account is just like a Business account. Like any bank account, Retailer has a legal right to Open JazzCash Retailer account.</p>

<p>&middot;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp; Retailer can request for JazzCash Retailer account opening by visiting Jazz Experience center, franchise.</p>

<p>&middot;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp; The franchise or jazz experience center will Inform the retailer the number of days required to open/ create retailer JazzCash account.</p>

<p>&middot;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp; Retailer can open only one JazzCash Retailer account on one CNIC number.</p>

<p>&middot;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp; If a retailer wants to create an account at another number, they must first close their existing account</p>

<p>&middot;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp; JazzCash Retailer account cannot be transferred to any other number</p>

<p>&middot;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp; But if you want to create an account on another number and don&#39;t want to get your account closed, then you can create another account on another CNIC number.</p>

<p>&middot;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp; As soon as the JazzCash retailer account is opened, the retailer receives a MPIN message</p>

<p>&middot;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp; If the retailer&#39;s MPIN message is deleted or not received, the retailer will call the helpline for the MPIN.</p>

<p>&middot;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp; There is no annual fee to use the JazzCash Retailer account</p>

<p>&middot;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp; Need to check via Retailer CNIC &amp; Same Calling MSISDN that account already exist or not</p>

<p>&middot;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp; To open a Retailer Account from Franchise/Business center, you must have a CNIC and Shop Name</p>

ðŸ“‹ ENTRY: JazzCash Retailer â€“ Account Status â€“ Sop
------------------------------------------------------------
Main Header: RTG
Network Provider: Jazz
Complaint Description: <p>&middot;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp; This process will cover call handling scenarios where Retailer is inquiring status of Account.</p>

<p>&middot;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp; This process provides general guidelines to handle account Status related calls.</p>

<p>&middot;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp; Account status is a value mentioned in CPS which shows the state of a Account.</p>

<p>&middot;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp; Each transaction status value has specific meaning which helps agent to identify the Account Status.</p>

<p>&middot;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp; Please refer to table 1.0 below for possible transaction statuses and their description.</p>

<p><strong>Table 1.0</strong></p>

<table border="1" cellpadding="0" cellspacing="0" style="width:595px">
	<tbody>
		<tr>
			<td style="vertical-align:top">
			<p><strong>Retailer Account Status value</strong></p>
			</td>
			<td style="vertical-align:top">
			<p><strong>Description</strong></p>
			</td>
		</tr>
		<tr>
			<td style="vertical-align:top">
			<p>Active</p>
			</td>
			<td style="vertical-align:top">
			<p>Where account registration completed but account MPIN Created and Account is ready for use.</p>
			</td>
		</tr>
		<tr>
			<td style="vertical-align:top">
			<p>Pending Active</p>
			</td>
			<td style="vertical-align:top">
			<p>Where account registration completed but account MPIN not Created.</p>
			</td>
		</tr>
		<tr>
			<td style="vertical-align:top">
			<p>Suspended</p>
			</td>
			<td style="vertical-align:top">
			<p>Two scenarios on which account marked as Suspend.</p>

			<p>&sect;&nbsp; Due to CNIC Expiry</p>

			<p>&sect;&nbsp; Due to fraudulent activity</p>
			</td>
		</tr>
		<tr>
			<td style="vertical-align:top">
			<p>Frozen</p>
			</td>
			<td style="vertical-align:top">
			<p>Two scenarios on which account marked as Frozen.</p>

			<p>&sect;&nbsp; In Deceased case till the settle of funds.</p>

			<p>&sect;&nbsp; Instruction by FIA/Court orders/ Fourth Schedule/NACTA on request of MMBL bank regulatory dept.</p>
			</td>
		</tr>
		<tr>
			<td style="vertical-align:top">
			<p>Closed</p>
			</td>
			<td style="vertical-align:top">
			<p>Closure request previously processed and marked closed no record in CPS.</p>
			</td>
		</tr>
	</tbody>
</table>

<p>&middot;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp; Agent will guide that customer will need to visit an agent to perform a biometric cash in to get the cash-in transaction activated</p>

<p>&middot;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp; Asaan Mobile Account is designed to allow individuals an easy gateway to mobile payments in Pakistan without having a smartphone or internet connectivity</p>

<p>&middot;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp; Now with a simple prompt of *2262#, you can open your Asaan Mobile Account and get your banking facility on your feature phone</p>

<p>&middot;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp; To link existing mobile account with USSD Dial *2262# &amp; select option 2 &ldquo;Mojooda mobile account ko USSD se link krein&rdquo;</p>

<p>&middot;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp; Asaan account is a service through which an individual can open an account. Asaan account enables low risk customers to perform any transaction without having a smartphone or internet connectivity</p>

<p>&sect;&nbsp; 4344 Self-Service</p>

<p>&sect;&nbsp; Jazz Point App</p>

<p>&sect;&nbsp; Via USSD</p>

<p><a name="_Hlk139326304">&middot;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp; <strong>For 4344 Service Only</strong></a></p>

<p>&middot;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp; If retailer sends invalid command he received message that include: &ldquo;You have provided invalid command valid Commands are:</p>

<p>&sect;&nbsp; D&nbsp;</p>

<p>&sect;&nbsp; M</p>

<p>&middot;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp; <strong>&quot;D&quot;</strong> for Previous Day <strong>&quot;M&quot;</strong> for 1st of current month till 12 AM last night</p>

<p>&sect;&nbsp; Current month Commission till last day as per below details:</p>

<p>&sect;&nbsp; Cash In=&gt; Count/Amount / Commission. This includes Cash-in and Money Transfer from CNIC to Mobile Account)</p>

<p>&sect;&nbsp; (Cash Out=&gt; Count/Amount / Commission)</p>

<p>&sect;&nbsp; (Collecting/Receiving =&gt; Count/Amount / Commission)</p>

<p>&sect;&nbsp; (CNIC Sending=&gt; Count/Amount / Commission) This includes Money Transfer from CNIC to CNIC only and reversals are not excluded</p>

<p>&sect;&nbsp; (Bank Deposit=&gt; Count/Amount / Commission)</p>

<p>&sect;&nbsp; (Utility Bill Payment=&gt; Count/Amount/Commission) This includes electricity, gas, PTCL Landline and water bill companies)</p>

<p>&middot;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp; <strong>4344 SMS Text:</strong></p>

<p>&sect;&nbsp; Trx= count/amount/commission</p>

<p>&sect;&nbsp; CI= 5/24,500/138</p>

<p>&sect;&nbsp; CO= 1/49,300/104</p>

<p>&sect;&nbsp; DR-R= 3/18,000/133</p>

<p>&sect;&nbsp; DR-S= 3/6,820/62</p>

<p>&sect;&nbsp; IBFT=1/50,000/124</p>

ðŸ“‹ ENTRY: JazzCash â€“ Retailer â€“ Customer Account Registration â€“ SOP
------------------------------------------------------------
Main Header: RTG
Network Provider: Jazz
Complaint Description: <p>&middot;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp; This SOP document will cover scenarios related with Customer Account Registration</p>

<p>&middot;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp; Customer Go to any nearby JazzCash Agent and get registered through our agents</p>

<p>&middot;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp; Customer can have 2 JazzCash account on one CNIC, one customer account and one merchant account on different MSISDN.</p>

<p>&middot;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp; Retailer can Registered the customer Account through BVS Device, and also registered the customer account via USSD menu *787#</p>

<p>&middot;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp; The customer will receive a flash message on their Jazz mobile number, asking them to reply with &ldquo;1&rdquo; to confirm Account registration. Once customer replies with 1, his/her account will be registered</p>

<p>&middot;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp; Customer will get a confirmation message from 8558 on provided JazzCash Account mobile number. Customer is requested to setup his/her MPIN by dialing *786# or using JazzCash App</p>

<p>&middot;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp; Retailer needs to make sure that customer&rsquo;s CNIC &amp; mobile is valid &amp; correct</p>

<p>&middot;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp; CNIC must not be expired. Retailer must get acknowledgement from customer before authorizing the transaction</p>

<p>&middot;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp; When taking fingerprints, it is recommended to start with the right thumb. The user may also take impressions of customer&rsquo;s left thumb, right index finger or left index finger; only one selection is required</p>

<p>&middot;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp; To ensure efficient verification by NADRA, the fingerprints must have a minimum of three green stars</p>

<p>&middot;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp; If Customer inquire about the Jazz Cash Customer Account feature. Retailer will ask to Customer route his relevant Jazz cash helpline (4444 / 042-111-124-444)</p>

ðŸ“‹ ENTRY: JazzCash â€“ Retailer â€“ Deposit Money â€“ SOP
------------------------------------------------------------
Main Header: RTG
Network Provider: Jazz
Complaint Description: <p>&middot;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp; This SOP document will cover scenarios related to Deposit Money.</p>

<p>&middot;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp; There are total <strong>3</strong> ways to Deposit Money in JazzCash account.</p>

<p>&sect;&nbsp; Deposit Money Through Jazz Franchise</p>

<p>&sect;&nbsp; Deposit Money Through Banks (Business Deposit)</p>

<p>&sect;&nbsp; Deposit Money Through Customer Account (Cash Out)</p>

<p><strong>Deposit Money Through Jazz Franchise</strong></p>

<p>&middot;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp; Retailer can deposit money through Jazz Franchise</p>

<p>&middot;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp; This deposit Money is also called B2B.</p>

<p>&middot;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp; Simply, provide your mobile number and cash to the Franchisee; money will be deposited into your JazzCash Retailer Account instantly</p>

<p><strong>Deposit Money Through Banks (Business Deposit)</strong></p>

<p>&middot;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp; Retailer can deposit money through Banks.</p>

<p>&sect;&nbsp; UBL</p>

<p>&sect;&nbsp; MCB</p>

<p>&sect;&nbsp; MMBL</p>

<p>&sect;&nbsp; ALFALAH BANK</p>

<p>&middot;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp; The service is free of charge for retailers with transaction Limit 500,000 per transaction (1.5 Million per day)</p>

<p>&middot;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp; For More details Refer to details Refer to JazzCash &ndash; Retailer &ndash; Business Deposit &ndash; SOP</p>

<p><strong>Deposit Money Through Customer Account (Cash Out)</strong></p>

<p>&middot;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp; Retailer can deposit money through Customer account</p>

<p>&middot;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp; This deposit Money is also called Cash Out.</p>

<p>&middot;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp; To withdraw cash, Customer provide his Mobile number to the Agent, confirm withdrawal with his MPIN and collect Cash</p>

<p>&middot;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp; Refer to <a name="_Hlk139326304">JazzCash &ndash; Retailer &ndash; Cash Out &ndash; SOP</a></p>

ðŸ“‹ ENTRY: JazzCash Retailer MSISDN Suspension by Authorized Official Employee
------------------------------------------------------------
Main Header: RTG
Network Provider: Jazz
Complaint Description: <p>&middot;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp; This SOP document will cover scenarios related to Retailer MSISDN Suspension.</p>

<p>&middot;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp; Attached File contains details of PMCL Employees Sales Team (Ams), Jazz DFS BDMs, Channel Support and DFS Channel Ops personals. These are the only persons who are authorized to call at 1344 helpline and can request to block retailer&rsquo;s MSISDN to control fraud or misuse of retailer funds.</p>

<p>&middot;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp; Agent will ask employee name and will also ask Franchise ID (need to verify only one franchise id) and will validate them in attach file.</p>

<p>&middot;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp; In attached file, multiple franchise IDs exists against authorized person and he/she can give any of the franchise ID to verify him/herself.</p>

<p>&middot;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp; If authorized person is from of DFS Teams (BDMs, Support or Channel Ops) in the attached sheet, they can provide franchisee ID that starts from 1, 8 and 9. If they provide any franchise ID that starts from 1, 8 and 9, agent will consider this as verified and will proceed with blocking the request.</p>

<p>&middot;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp; Helpline Representative will perform blocking of retailer MSISDN immediately.</p>

<p>&middot;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp; While blocking agent must enter &ldquo;Blocking on Behalf of Retailer by Caller/Employee name (AM/BDMs/DFS Channel Ops), and will mention Calling CLI.</p>

<p>&middot;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp; Restoration will be done as per existing process via Regional team acknowledgement by Fin Digital team/FRMU/FRM/DFS Ops after successful Sim replacement done by retailer<a name="_Hlk139326304">.</a></p>

<p>&nbsp;</p>

<p><span style="font-size:11pt"><span style="font-family:Calibri,sans-serif"><strong><u><span style="font-size:12.0pt">How to Generate a Voucher via USSD Menu</span></u></strong><strong><u><span style="font-size:12.0pt">:</span></u></strong></span></span></p>

<ul>
	<li><span style="font-size:11pt"><span style="font-family:Calibri,sans-serif">Dial *787#.</span></span></li>
	<li><span style="font-size:11pt"><span style="font-family:Calibri,sans-serif">Select &quot;Initiate Haball Payment&quot;.</span></span></li>
	<li><span style="font-size:11pt"><span style="font-family:Calibri,sans-serif">Select &quot;Retailer Deposit&quot;.</span></span></li>
	<li><span style="font-size:11pt"><span style="font-family:Calibri,sans-serif">Enter the amount.</span></span></li>
	<li><span style="font-size:11pt"><span style="font-family:Calibri,sans-serif">Re-enter the amount.</span></span></li>
	<li><span style="font-size:11pt"><span style="font-family:Calibri,sans-serif">Enter your MPIN.</span></span></li>
	<li><span style="font-size:11pt"><span style="font-family:Calibri,sans-serif">The deposit request will be successfully sent; visit the nearest bank or portal to complete the deposit.</span></span></li>
	<li><span style="font-size:11pt"><span style="font-family:Calibri,sans-serif">The retailer will receive a confirmation SMS.</span></span></li>
</ul>

<p style="margin-left:48px">&nbsp;</p>

<p><span style="font-size:11pt"><span style="font-family:Calibri,sans-serif"><strong><u><span style="font-size:12.0pt">Method to Deposit Retailer Funds</span></u></strong><strong><u><span style="font-size:12.0pt">:</span></u></strong></span></span></p>

<p><span style="font-size:11pt"><span style="font-family:Calibri,sans-serif"><strong><span style="font-size:12.0pt">Bank Counter Method</span></strong><strong><span style="font-size:12.0pt">:</span></strong></span></span></p>

<ul>
	<li><span style="font-size:11pt"><span style="font-family:Calibri,sans-serif">Fill in the Haball payment receipt and enter the <strong>18-digit voucher ID</strong> and <strong>amount</strong>.</span></span></li>
	<li><span style="font-size:11pt"><span style="font-family:Calibri,sans-serif">After filling the Haball payment slip, visit the nearest <strong>bank branch</strong>.</span></span></li>
	<li><span style="font-size:11pt"><span style="font-family:Calibri,sans-serif">Provide the <strong>Haball payment slip</strong> to the bank cashier and deposit the funds.</span></span></li>
	<li><span style="font-size:11pt"><span style="font-family:Calibri,sans-serif">The bank will confirm the deposit, and the <strong>amount will be credited</strong> to the retailer&rsquo;s account.</span></span></li>
	<li><span style="font-size:11pt"><span style="font-family:Calibri,sans-serif">The retailer will receive a <strong>confirmation SMS</strong>.</span></span></li>
</ul>

<p><span style="font-size:11pt"><span style="font-family:Calibri,sans-serif"><strong><span style="font-size:12.0pt">Mobile App Method</span></strong><strong><span style="font-size:12.0pt">:</span></strong></span></span></p>

<ul>
	<li><span style="font-size:11pt"><span style="font-family:Calibri,sans-serif">Log in to any of the above-mentioned bank <strong>mobile apps</strong>.</span></span></li>
	<li><span style="font-size:11pt"><span style="font-family:Calibri,sans-serif">Select <strong>&quot;Payment/Corporate&quot;</strong>.</span></span></li>
	<li><span style="font-size:11pt"><span style="font-family:Calibri,sans-serif">Choose the <strong>&quot;Haball&quot;</strong> option.</span></span></li>
	<li><span style="font-size:11pt"><span style="font-family:Calibri,sans-serif">Enter the <strong>voucher code (</strong><strong>received via </strong><strong>SMS)</strong> and complete the deposit.</span></span></li>
	<li><span style="font-size:11pt"><span style="font-family:Calibri,sans-serif">The retailer will receive a <strong>confirmation SMS</strong>.</span></span></li>
</ul>

<p><span style="font-size:11pt"><span style="font-family:Calibri,sans-serif"><strong><u><span style="font-size:12.0pt">How to Check Voucher Status via USSD Menu</span></u></strong><strong><u><span style="font-size:12.0pt">:</span></u></strong></span></span></p>

<ul>
	<li><span style="font-size:11pt"><span style="font-family:Calibri,sans-serif">Dial *787#.</span></span></li>
	<li><span style="font-size:11pt"><span style="font-family:Calibri,sans-serif">Select &quot;Retailer Deposit&quot;.</span></span></li>
	<li><span style="font-size:11pt"><span style="font-family:Calibri,sans-serif">Select &quot;Haball Payment&quot;.</span></span></li>
	<li><span style="font-size:11pt"><span style="font-family:Calibri,sans-serif">Select &quot;Check Status&quot;.</span></span></li>
	<li><span style="font-size:11pt"><span style="font-family:Calibri,sans-serif">Enter the Voucher ID (PSID).</span></span></li>
	<li><span style="font-size:11pt"><span style="font-family:Calibri,sans-serif">The status of the voucher will appear on the screen, and you will receive an SMS confirmation.</span></span></li>
</ul>

<p><span style="font-size:11pt"><span style="font-family:Calibri,sans-serif"><strong><u><span style="font-size:12.0pt">How to Check Voucher Status via USSD Menu</span></u></strong><strong><u><span style="font-size:12.0pt">:</span></u></strong></span></span></p>

<ul>
	<li><span style="font-size:11pt"><span style="font-family:Calibri,sans-serif">Dial *787#.</span></span></li>
	<li><span style="font-size:11pt"><span style="font-family:Calibri,sans-serif">Select &quot;Retailer Deposit&quot;.</span></span></li>
	<li><span style="font-size:11pt"><span style="font-family:Calibri,sans-serif">Select &quot;Haball Payment&quot;.</span></span></li>
	<li><span style="font-size:11pt"><span style="font-family:Calibri,sans-serif">Select &quot;Cancel Haball Payment&quot;.</span></span></li>
	<li><span style="font-size:11pt"><span style="font-family:Calibri,sans-serif">Enter the Voucher ID (PSID).</span></span></li>
	<li><span style="font-size:11pt"><span style="font-family:Calibri,sans-serif">Enter your 4-digit MPIN to confirm</span></span></li>
	<li><span style="font-size:11pt"><span style="font-family:Calibri,sans-serif">The retailer will receive a <strong>confirmation SMS</strong>.</span></span></li>
</ul>
